	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') != 'd44e920c3314995f798bbdca25126f0e39fddf6a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== 'd44e920c3314995f798bbdca25126f0e39fddf6a') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== '7c5f298fb8e1b23d1005d1264938961209f6c1a9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/run.inc.php') !== 'd44e920c3314995f798bbdca25126f0e39fddf6a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/run.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_access.sql') !== '5d91697edc4a09239e439d682299536e50dd9134') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_access.sql');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	writefile_16();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') != 'bba035815ce0298d89d92fbac2312f23f34931e8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'bba035815ce0298d89d92fbac2312f23f34931e8') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'b5e110c81a1a57427d3301f60f09e3a50a2e9f18') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'bba035815ce0298d89d92fbac2312f23f34931e8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql') != '48fa4bc15639e0919536f89ef4b1073eb5f4cfd3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql') !== '48fa4bc15639e0919536f89ef4b1073eb5f4cfd3') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql') !== '438ee457b630a793e8edcb61bfca0832c09f9a84') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql') !== '48fa4bc15639e0919536f89ef4b1073eb5f4cfd3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mysql.sql');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_oracle.sql');

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_oracle.sql');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') != 'b126ad6cb2d981b42d69a7a091a2b8d1b38590f8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== 'b126ad6cb2d981b42d69a7a091a2b8d1b38590f8') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== 'f1f09c4d3e63c5d268a1bf7c590951dd0cc45b4d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== 'b126ad6cb2d981b42d69a7a091a2b8d1b38590f8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
		}
	}
